                   President of the World Peace Unification Family Association, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
Hope of the Youth
I know that you have been quite tired from your activities over the past few days. From now on, I am thinking of having activities until ten o'clock at night and extending the time for rest when you return to the headquarters. So I hope you will do that. You might be thinking, "Oh, I should go out and work hard, but why is the teacher appearing so early in the morning?" But I would like to ask for a little time. Let's talk for a moment about the topic of "Hope of the Youth." 

The greater the hope and ideals a young person has, the more they must possess the ability to take initiative. No young person would want to miss the chance to become a global figure and to shape the world according to their will. I believe that for most people, the period from adolescence to their thirties is a time when such dreams can soar high. Therefore, to carve out such a place during adolescence, it is absolutely necessary to have a solid foundation within oneself.

So, I think about how wonderful it would be if every household could provide such an environment. Then, I think about how great it would be if one's parents were influential figures in the country or in the world. If not, how wonderful it would be if one's older brother or sister could be such a foundation. This is a common way of thinking, centering on one's closest relatives.

In this way, everyone thinks that they would like their home to be the center of the nation and the world. However, if such an environment is established, the real question is whether I can become a central figure in the world and move the world. It is easy to think only about external circumstances. Therefore, the ultimate issue is that, no matter how favorable the environment may be, I do not consider myself to be the problem. Furthermore, when I find myself in such a position, I do not think about whether I am capable of inheriting the historical legacy.

Now, when you think about it, if you stand on a historical foundation and receive a realistic foundation, can you really do it? If you have excellent parents and excellent siblings, can you be better than them? This becomes a realistic issue that you confront.

Since all problems arise from this point, the conclusion is that you must learn and study to solve these problems. You must learn. You must strive.

First of all, from a practical standpoint, no matter how excellent your parents or older siblings may be, the question is whether they can present content that automatically and theoretically agrees with my suggestions and claims, and whether they can be the subject that can put those theoretical claims into practice. We must recognize that there are important issues that need to be resolved based on the foundation of a single household.

Externally, the same applies. There will be opposing groups as well. Since not everything happens freely, there will be many conflicts. The question then is whether you have the subjective ability to digest these conflicts and the standards of your own self to lead.

From this perspective, no matter how capable you are, how knowledgeable you are, or how patient you are, the issue of how to establish a worldview that the world can look up to from your family is an extremely significant problem. If such a problem is not established, no matter how wonderful your home is, or even if it is a royal palace, it will inevitably be replaced according to the historical environment.

From this perspective, when you truly think about wanting to serve the world and to become a truly global figure, it is important to establish an ideological subjectivity that can govern the history that develops through the past, present, and future without being swept away by history.

To create a world centered on God is the highest ideal. Young people should not only have dreams of humanity. Humans are bound to change. Change is brought about through ideology. The development of science is all based on formulas, applying those formulas and developing according to the results. Today's modern civilization is based on that. Similarly, can humans not have ideals that can apply some formal principles? Ultimately, a person of character must be a formal figure who can encompass the past, present, and future.

Then, who establishes that formula? If it is established among humans, there is no way other than for the intellectuals of the world to come together and create an association to establish formulas. However, if there is an absolute God, if there is some causal being that transcends humanity, we must consider whether the formulas established by that causal being and those established by humans can be the same. From this perspective, you must understand that those who propose formulas among humans are unaware of the future.

Therefore, a formal character must transcend history. In other words, the standard must be established in such a way that it can observe the future and the past and present. This leads to the conclusion that it is reasonable for people to seek a personal standard centered on God.

From this perspective, we can understand that a personal standard is established by God. From there, there can be an ideal family, an ideal society, an ideal nation, and an ideal world; it cannot be established with the ideal types that changing humans create as methods to break through their realities. Therefore, thoughtful young people or young people with dreams must conclude and organize their ideological and cognitive reasoning.

The ideal world is a world for the world, and the ideology of the ideal world is undoubtedly an ideology for a world that will remain unchanged forever in the future. Within that ideology, all people can possess the same formal value.

Today, in the medical field, a drug called penicillin has been developed, which works for Western people but not for Eastern people or Black people. That is not the case; it works universally for everyone. From this perspective, the ideologies that people around the world advocate today should not be one-sided. They must have content that can represent the whole, that can bring everyone into the realm of value, and that can bring joy to all.

Today, communism speaks of a dictatorial regime for workers and farmers. Also, in today's democratic world, the Christian ideology is not achieving equality. Racial discrimination still exists.

Now, we can conclude that the ideals and ideologies we are currently advocating are in the process of reaching a destination that we have not yet reached.

So, what is the ultimate ideal and ideology that youth can hope for? It is the pursuit of a value-based world that can equalize all people centered on the absolute God. This is the path humanity must take.

From this, we conclude that a system centered on God is necessary. Therefore, the issue is between God and me. Thus, we must recognize that what humanity needs in the future is a religion that completely unites God and me.

There are only two ways to achieve unity between God and me through that religion. Wouldn't it be wonderful if there were a way for God to completely unite with me? If such a way exists, everyone would say, "I will take this path." Young people tend to think that way. If so, that is good. God says, "Whatever is good, I will go. But can you be more than me?" That is where the problem lies. Can you do that? "No." Ultimately, you must realize that you do not possess the content that can be the subject itself, and you cannot complete the purpose as a subject and present the world of value.

Therefore, a wise youth would throw everything away and say, "I will serve you as the subject, so please command me." This method is concluded to be the best method.

The Unification Church seeks to unite God and humanity. So, what do we, the youth of the Unification Church, want to do? "Let’s see if God and humanity can become one." This is undoubtedly the goal. Isn't it true? "Yes." Is it "God, come to us," or "We will go to God"? What is it? "We will go to God." We must recognize that this is where the Unification Church differs from traditional churches.

Christianity prays, "Oh! Our Christianity has laid the foundation around the world, so God, come down and work with us. Bless us." However, the omniscient and omnipotent God knows everything. He knows that it would be futile to try, so He does not move.

If the members of traditional churches are going this way, and God says, "Turn back!" can they turn back? They only know one way. They do not know that there are East and West, North and South. However, the Unification Church is different. If God says, "Turn back!" they will turn back. The Unification Church may tell you to study, to work, to fight, to make money, and to do all sorts of things. "Oh, I want to be like this, but this is unsuitable for me..." Then, ideals and everything else become meaningless. There is nothing.

If you are young, if you are a youth, you should have a passionate hope and a strong conviction, and even if you cannot be the subject, you should be able to digest that subject. Discovering how to find that self is what I consider a wise discovery.

If God exists, what would He desire? What would it be? This is where the will of God becomes an issue. What is the will of God? The will of God is to save the world. It is to create a world that aligns with God's heart.

So, what should we do? "Oh! There is God's heart and my heart, so let’s compromise and do it." Can we do that? "No." Therefore, we must probe into God's heart here. We must understand that God likes what is public and good.

Then, how do we know what is public and good? Even the most evil person knows what is public and good. If there is someone who is innocent, and a hundred or a thousand people attack them, which is public: standing with a hundred or a thousand people, or standing with one person? You must understand the meaning of what is public. In a world of general sin, people may consider a hundred people to be public, but historically, the one person who stands to represent the whole from a position of goodness is the public person. You must recognize that that one person has a historical mission to establish an absolute public standard.

When I am suffering like this, for whom am I suffering? Am I suffering for myself, for the future world, for the nation, or for true people? From this perspective, suffering for others is public. You must understand that what is public remains forever. Why? Because I am sacrificed, but it remains in all directions. My public good can remain in all directions.

Next, what is good? It is to wish for blessings while being sacrificed. Just like Jesus prayed while dying on the cross... that is the higher good. These things cannot be occupied by the past, present, or future. They are dominated by them and cannot dominate or subjugate them.

Now, where is your heart trying to go? Do you want to be on the side of the hundred people who are attacking, or on the side of the one person who is right? "On the side of the one person who is right." Then, is the Unification Church a bad religious organization or a good one? Or is Reverend Moon a bad person or a good person? We must understand these things.

Young people should have public, true, and good hopes. Does the teacher teach you to fight? Does he say, "Hit back, hit back"? An evil person teaches to hit back twice when someone hits them once. That is evil. There is a difference. There is a difference. Right now, America is opposing us, and the media is making a fuss against us, but we remain calm. We are calm, right? Aren't you all calm now? Does that match the feelings of young people? Does it match or not?

The teacher's temperament is like that. He is someone who likes to smash things with one hit. He is originally someone who likes that. (Laughter) He does not lose to anyone. Then, this is a training process. It is to cultivate the disposition to fight against the world, so we are undergoing training. However, God does not test us through the members of the Unification Church. You must understand that God tests us through external people, through the side of Satan. Therefore, the whole of America opposes us, the entire church opposes us, and those who used to follow the Unification Church are all put in a position of opposition.

What is the purpose of this testing? To create a counterpart like God... You must understand that. Until now, whether people have opposed God or not, whether the whole world has said various things about God, no matter how many pastors or priests who followed God oppose Him, God remains calm. In the midst of that opposition, He does not despair; rather, He is not captured.
is not about that, but rather the fact that we must recognize the hope for the future that exists there. That is what is great. No matter how much chaos ensues and how much we struggle at the brink of death, we must understand that the thought that there is a hope that can be revered more than our own lives is what is great. "This hope is not a hope that can be achieved by fighting alongside you, so I endure!" This is the lesson we have. How wonderful is that? How magnificent is that?

Similarly, everyone, if all the youth of the Unification Church are making a fuss saying, "Oh, what is this? Waking up at five-thirty, not even having time to eat, busy going to the bathroom, and even when letters come from my parents, I have no time to write back to my hometown. What is this? I can't live like this." If you look at it like that, it will be astonishing. Whether it’s washing underwear or whatever... But we must understand this. If there is sweat or dirt on a body that possesses God's unchanging hope and peace, that time is a holy time, a holy time. If the underwear is dirty, that is holy underwear. We must recognize that it is called 'holy.' That time is holy. Even if the underwear is torn and smells, it is holy underwear. (Laughter) Do you understand what I mean?

There was a time when I also had dirt on my hands, and if I scratched with five fingers, lines would appear. However, when I looked at it later, I saw that it was shining, shining. That is what is holy. Therefore, what is public, true, and good shines and becomes holy the more we suffer and sacrifice. It is holy.

When we think about such things, I was born from a sinful lineage, and I am currently a sinner, but if there is a way for my sinful self to be holy, then there is no more glorious and miraculous event than that. Could it not be concluded that even Jesus, while shedding blood at such a level, could praise his own holiness? Do you understand? Do you know what I mean? "Yes."

Then, what kind of hope should our young people in this world have? We can conclude that we must have God's precious, true, good, and public hope. 

Everyone, in that sense, all the members of the Unification Church, whether it is the teacher or all of you, even if we stand in the midst of opposition from the world and opposition from all over America, as long as God is alive, this organization will not perish. Only in such a place can the world of hope emerge, and only here can God's will be fulfilled. Therefore, it is an obvious conclusion that it cannot be achieved without a public foundation, without a foundation of goodness.

The hope of the Unification Church for the nation and the world is a hope that will last forever. Earlier, I mentioned that youth need a foundation established by their parents that is globally centered. Now, let’s think about a foundation centered on God, centered on the Unification Church. Our Unification Church, centered on the eternal will of God, centered on the eternal love of God, is a group that hopes for a nation transcending ethnicity, hopes for a kingdom transcending the world, and cries out for true parents and true siblings in the family. This is an astonishing fact. And as we move forward, it is not for my own prosperity, but for the sake of the nation and the world that we dedicate everything. This is an astonishing revolution. It is a remarkable historical revolution that we must recognize.

I have thought based on such history and have laid this historical foundation. However, no matter how much America stands before God's will, Reverend Moon has no intention of settling down and living well in America. I think of going to the remote areas of Africa. What America needs is to save that country quickly.

Young men and women of the Unification Church, do you have hope? "Yes." What kind of hope is it? It is not the hope of young people that has been rotting on the ground until now. You must know that it is a hope that will last forever. Therefore, I am a thinker, a person of intellect, and a person of ability, but I dedicate my whole life to this play. That is because this is more valuable than anything in the world, and you must understand that I am engaging in this play while traversing the realm of life and death.

Do you want to be a tiger cub or a kitten? "A tiger cub." "Well, that's what the teacher says, but I can't do it." Those who say that are kittens, kittens. Kittens look for mouse holes and go into corners, but tiger cubs go up high. Even as cubs, they go up high. If it’s New York, they go to the top of New York. (Applause) They go to the top of NBC, the top of the New York Times. Kittens run away the more obstacles there are, but tiger cubs rise and rise. (Roar) (Laughter)

If a tiger moves, it swallows everything whole. When I move, I swallow everything whole. You little brats! Are you the same? "Yes." If you are out on the street saying, "Oh, what about this and that? Oh, I got a ticket again today. What is this?" and scratching your head, you are not a tiger cub. From now on, I will think, "It keeps getting hotter! It keeps getting hotter!" The sun is shining down, making the youth of the Unification Church sweat more. How wonderful is it to work in the heat? Do you understand what I mean? That’s how I am thinking. This little thing is not a problem. "The king of sweat flows down like this." You must be able to say that. (Laughter) Isn’t that right? That’s what it is.

Then, do you want to meet God? How about it, do you really want to meet God? "Yes." How would you like to meet Him? Would you like to meet Him straight on, or would you like to meet Him sideways? "Straight on." What do you think God would think? Would He want to meet you just a little bit sideways? It’s the same. When He meets you, He wants to meet you like this. Nose to nose. You are the same, and God is the same. (Applause) That is the law of God. You must understand that God desires that.

Young people of the Unification Church who are to inherit the heavenly enterprise, wouldn’t it be nice if God appeared when you pray and said, "You rascal!" and gives you orders every day? "Yes." When you see, "Oh, God, give me strength! Give me strength!" I often feel pity for you. (Laughter)

When you stand behind God and say, "God, let me meet You," would God want to meet you? God is saying, "Hey! Come here, come here. Come back, come back, come back." You must understand that.

That is why when you pray, don’t do it desperately, exhausted, saying, "God, give me strength!" Instead, you should pray gloriously, putting all your effort into it, "God, give me the strength to fight again!" That is how you should pray. You must go out stronger, stronger. You must understand that only then will God help you. That is the attitude of wanting to meet God face to face.

If you cannot work... I cannot pray if I cannot work. I would rather sleep. I don’t pray. I am too ashamed... However, when facing opposition and difficult situations, I need strength, so I can pray, "God, I must go further." If you have this thought every hour, even while working, you will feel insufficient. Even while working, you will feel insufficient. You must have the heart that cannot pray, saying, "I must do more. I must do more." If you go out like this every day, God will surely guide you. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." But if you are struggling and saying, "Oh!" God sees that and it is utterly miserable.

Now look at our Unification Church. Does the foundation of the Unification Church envy the foundation of an American senator? Does it envy the foundation of the President of the United States? What do you envy? Do you envy that? "No." Isn’t it more than that? I am trying to save the President of the United States, I am trying to teach the American senators, I am trying to lead the American people; the Unification Church has no thought of being led. So, do I need it? Do I need it? "Yes." If that is the case in America, which leads the world, then what is there to envy in the world?

Now, look. Who made these American youths like this? Can a president make them? Can a senator make them? Can any religious leader make someone say, "I will work even if I die"? Who can make that happen? You must understand what kind of place this is. You must now recognize the astonishing fact that the youth can have hope in an environment that is established, a wonderful environment.

Now the problem is you yourself. The foundation is all there. From this foundation, how much effort do you have to convince the teacher, convince the leader, and convince your brothers in the Unification Church? That is what will determine whether you inherit this great heavenly enterprise or not.

You will become a son or daughter who is praised by your parents or siblings. Will you become a son or daughter who is criticized? "Praised..." Is that really so? "Yes." Then when you go out to work in New York, will you be someone who only works in one place? Or will you be someone who sweeps across all of New York? What will it be? At a glance, your eyes should sparkle. The symbol of America is the eagle, and you must understand that the expression of that bird, the bird that eats others, should be "big."

Raise your hand if you are American. Put it down. The white-headed eagle of America is the most vicious eagle. You must understand that the characteristic of that eagle is that it has the trait of snatching food from other eagles that are carrying it. Do you understand that? "Yes." That is why they conquered the Indian nations. So, I think that is the kind of eagle I have created. In the same way, we want to snatch people from the world of Satan, who are being taken away. If you think of it that way, I think it is a wonderful symbol.

So, don’t just eat what you have, but raise it and have offspring to eat. That’s what it means. (Laughter) Can you do that? "Yes." Now, I think you understand.

The only organization that can save this fallen world is the Unification Church. 

If you are a youth, you have dreams. You have hope. Our dream is to hold God in our right hand and the world in our left hand. Is it wonderful to hold God and everything else and move forward? Is it wonderful to just hold onto people? Which is better? "The former." Which is better, to abandon the world and just hold onto God? "The former." The Christian thought is the central thought of the democratic world, which says to hold onto God and abandon the world. Communism says to abandon God and just hold onto the world. The Unification Church is to unify these two, to hold onto God and hold onto the world. Which is better? "The Unification Church." You must understand that.

Therefore, we must endure more hardships than the difficulties faced by the democratic world, and we must endure more hardships than those faced by the communist world. Otherwise, we cannot create one. If we are less than communism, we cannot fulfill our purpose. If we are less than Christians, we cannot fulfill our purpose. If we are smaller than the combined strength of both, we cannot fulfill our purpose. We must be greater than the combined strength of communism and democracy. Therefore, it is an obvious conclusion that even if established churches and communism go, the only thing that will remain is the Unification Church. That day is not far off.

Now, established churches are collapsing. Communism is also collapsing. What about the Unification Church? "No." Right now, a sprout is coming out. The roots are more than enough to cover the world. Can communism uproot this? Can Christianity uproot this? "No." Just wait and see when the time comes. In three years, four years, five years, just wait and see in ten years.

Now, do you have dreams? Do you have hope? To the young men and women of the Unification Church gathered here, do you have dreams and hope? "Yes." With one foot, you must step on the democratic world, and with the other foot, you must step on the communist world, and you must be able to hold God with both hands. If it is a dream of young people, there is no better dream than this. If there is hope, there is no peak of hope greater than this.

Then the question is how can I become a subjective being who can digest this? Even if the wind blows and the storm approaches, I cannot retreat. I can retreat one step to the left, but I cannot retreat to the right. You must understand that. Do you agree? "Yes." The attitude of a man who has such hope and such dreams is to stand on a rock and take an unchanging position. Only a young person who can take such a position can keep dreams and hopes alive. Bring on the typhoon! Even if I fly away, I will become a rubber band that stretches.

Are you that strong? "Yes." What about the women? "Yes." The weak one is the woman. Do women want to be like that? "Yes." Do you want to not fly away when the typhoon comes? "Yes." I will now send you to the brothels of New York City and make all the men come back. Can you do that? "Yes." Even if your legs are shaking, (gesturing) can you still go? (Laughter) And these men must go to the brothels and bring all the women back. Can you do that? "Yes." Raise your hand if you are willing to do that. If so, I will buy a house there right away and set up a headquarters. (Applause)

We have a dream that can swallow even the world of Satan. We must first swallow Satan before we can swallow God. Then God will naturally appear.

Women must repent the three men who are like archangels in this world. You must understand that you have that responsibility.

The three eras of the Old Testament, New Testament, and Completed Testament have passed to find the sun. Why? Because we are looking for the sun. We have gone through three eras to find the sun. The archangel Satan behind you has betrayed God over three eras. He is the enemy, the enemy. Therefore, to become the original sun that faced the three archangels, we must lead three people who can absolutely obey.

Therefore, no matter how handsome a man may be, no matter how charming he may be, he must remain steadfast. He must remain steadfast. Women, can you do that? "Yes." If you can do that, raise your hand. Wow, you are more wonderful than me. (Laughter)

On the other hand, men represent Adam and have gone through the fallen Adam restoration era, consuming the Old Testament era, the New Testament era, and the Completed Testament era... They have not established the authority of men after going through three eras without having women.
Because of this, you need to find a woman. In the end, Eve is just like a prostitute. She is a prostitute. Therefore, you need to enter the brothel. Can you do it?  
"Yes." Raise your hand if you want to go. You kids, if you create that headquarters and bring everyone here, open the doors all around and give them freedom until midnight, I would like to see what happens.  
Whether America can be saved or not depends on whether we can correct the issue of youth prostitution today. Furthermore, whether the Unification Church can take responsibility for that depends on whether it has the subjective authority or not.  
That is why, in order not to become a dropout in this society and to become a victor, I must undergo all kinds of training. I must undergo all kinds of training. We are not foolish. Just like Eve and Adam in the past, we will not be deceived. You all agree, right? "Yes." Then the problem is simple. If we cannot correct this, your sons and daughters will end up like that. Your sons and daughters will become like that.  
Who will take responsibility for that? Religious organizations should take responsibility, but which religious organization will do it? Established churches cannot do it. With the military power of America, or with political power, it cannot be done. Not even with atomic bombs. It cannot be done. The only one left is the Unification Church. You need to understand that the organization that can give hope is the Unification Church.  
When this breaks down, the hopes of young people will all be shattered. Therefore, you need to have a subjective ideology that can digest everything in such a world. Young people, the youth of the Unification Church must have dreams and hopes, but if they cannot digest this, all hope and dreams will disappear. We must let the American people know our intentions, and if you cannot save America, you need to understand that you will lose the democratic world.  
The youth of the Unification Church must take responsibility for the issues of prostitution, communism, and Christianity.  
So, shall we start with the easy things, or shall we tackle the hardest things first? What do you think? "The hardest things first." We must tackle the three hardest things. What is one of them? It is taking responsibility for the issue of youth prostitution worldwide. This is a monster that disrupts God's will, an enemy.  
And the foundation of Christianity, which has been prepared for 6,000 years, has collapsed globally, so we must revive Christianity. This is the hardest and most frightening thing. This is what God is most troubled about.  
Next is communism. Look, America cannot handle this, nor can any other country. No religion can handle this. So can the Unification Church do it or not? "Yes."  
Our young men and women must create a thorough model regarding the issue of gender. We must establish standards and create a traditional foundation. Can you all do that? "Yes."  
You need to know the amazing fact that families from Japan can live together for five years, sleeping under the same blanket, without engaging in relations. Young men and women of America, can you do that? "Yes." Only we can prevent the problem of youth prostitution. If the Unification Church cannot do it, the world will flow away. You need to understand that it will break and perish.  
When you look at the churches in America, there are no young people, right? So I think we need to make young people like us and send them all to church. Then who will take responsibility for guarding against the threat of communism? You need to know that our brothers are risking their lives fighting underground in the Iron Curtain or communist countries. There was a time when someone sent a letter to the teacher saying, "Teacher, the end is approaching, and I will meet you in the spirit world." We need to understand that we are in such a struggle. Who will defend against communism? Isn’t it just us?  
So when Reverend Moon says he will save these youth, the prostitutes are protesting. They are protesting... They are opposing Reverend Moon and the Unification Church, saying they want to save the established churches. They are also opposing when he says he will save them from communism.  
So, should we stop because they oppose us? Should we halt, or should we advance? "We should advance." Even if my life is at stake? Even if my neck is on the line? "Yes." We need to understand that we are prepared to sacrifice our lives in this struggle. So, if the teacher dies, can you uphold the teacher's ideology and die with him? "Yes." When Jesus went to the cross, did all twelve disciples run away? Even if you don’t say it, more than 80% of you would be that way. "No." I cannot believe that. When Jesus told Peter, "You will deny me three times," how determined was Peter when he said, "I will not do that even if I die"?  
Therefore, if you do not want to be that kind of person, fight with your life from now on. Fight with your life. You must fight as if you are already dead. There is no other way. If you are such people, if you are young people with such dreams and hopes, you can turn hell into heaven, and you can automatically establish heaven. Then you will become victors of both worlds. The teacher has been anticipating this for over 30 years and has been preparing for this path until now.  
So, you must understand that the only organization that can save Christianity is the Unification Church, logically and theoretically... Isn’t that right? It is certain. It is an undeniable fact that we are the only ones who can correct the youth. That is why we hold the Blessing Ceremony in the Unification Church. We conduct international marriages that transcend nations. Do you all have such thoughts? "Yes."  
Furthermore, the only one who fights against communism with their life until the end as an anti-communist in Asia and globally is Reverend Moon alone. The only ones fighting in Germany and Asia are us.  
When thinking about this, if you truly have dreams and hopes as youth, where will you work? Where will you go? Is there anywhere else to go? You need to understand that the only place to go is the Unification Church, the Unification Church.

**Principle of Cain's Restoration**
Recognizing Cain's position and abilities, we must treat him as a king, a father, and an elder brother, so that Cain will be willing to obey and submit to Abel. If not, he will not submit. Abel must serve Cain with a joyful heart, rejoicing in all that Cain is, for true submission comes from such a heart. 
If Abel does not serve with a joyful heart, it cannot be called true service. Only when served in this way does it become glorious service, free of repercussions. 
After that, Abel can command Cain. Commands must be given for the benefit of Cain, so that he will follow. If a king commands, "Serve me," the people will not only refuse to serve but will rebel. However, if the command is for the people, they will joyfully obey. 
When a father teaches a child, when an elder brother teaches a younger brother, or when a school teacher teaches students, they must not teach them to become inferior beings. The principle is that they should teach them to become better than themselves, to become superior individuals. This mindset must be eliminated. 
Abel should not pray for himself but must pray for Cain. When the teacher was in Hungnam prison, he did not pray for himself but fervently prayed for the family members in the South. He prayed, calling each of their names, knowing that they had left. 
June 6, 1976, East Garden, New York. 
* This message was given right after the Yankee Stadium event and is included in the 12th issue of <Ministry>.

In raising a child, parents should not assert their position loudly. They must care for the child's dirty and ugly urine and feces so that later, when the child grows up, they will serve their parents. 
Who do parents exist for? They exist for their children. How can one be a father without children, or a teacher without students? A commoner must treat a noble well for the noble to act as one; otherwise, how can a noble act as one? 
One must not take a high position as Abel and command Cain to do this or that. Such leaders are bound to fail. One must dedicate oneself to Cain, even if it means staying up all night for him, and must sacrifice their life ahead of Cain. Even if Cain retreats, Abel cannot retreat. 
Cain is in the position of an archangel and is the actual ruler. He was the actual ruler even before the fall. He was the actual ruler who evenly distributed all love coming from God. After the fall, he has continued to hold and exercise that power even more. We must respect such a ruler and recognize his value for restoration to gradually occur. 
Wherever God is present, Cain and Abel must be united. Therefore, heart and body, Cain and Abel, subject and object must become one for the purpose to be accomplished. Without God’s presence, nothing can be achieved. God being with us means that Cain and Abel have become one. Abel must not be alone in a state of confusion. If Cain and Abel do not unite, Satan will invade, and the purpose cannot be fulfilled. 
Respect and love Cain. If you force him to submit, he will always want to leave. Did not the Korean people, who were oppressed by Japan, look forward to the day of liberation? Coercion may provide the power to restore externally, but not internally. 
Restoration must be through love. Complete restoration cannot happen without love. One who has lost love has lost God. Therefore, if one has lost love, it is evidence that they have lost God. 

**Me and God**
You all know that now that the Yankee Stadium event is over, we must advance toward the Washington event. Probably, everyone will have to depart tomorrow. So, where will you go? You must all go according to the responsibilities assigned to you. Therefore, today, let’s briefly talk about 'Me and the Whole' or 'Me and God.' 
Everyone tends to think centered around themselves. 
Among the people gathered here, there are white people, black people, yellow people, and various races. Black individuals think, "I am of the black world." White individuals think, "I am of the white world," and yellow individuals think, "I am of the yellow world." 
Moreover, within white countries, there are various nations, and within black countries, there are various nations, and within yellow countries, there are various nations. Even among white countries, there is "our country," among black countries, there is "our country," and among yellow countries, there is "our country." When there are organizations centered around their own countries or families, people always think of themselves first. 
When thinking like this, people start from the whole, gradually getting smaller, and ultimately, what do they prioritize? They cannot remove 'me.' They cannot remove 'me.' In a broad view, this world contains various ethnic groups, but within that world, it becomes 'me.' No matter how small it is, even if it gets smaller centered around 'me,' they do not want to shift that focal point. This applies to both men and women. 
There is a small baby named Kwon Jin, and in the morning, when everyone gathers, he hopes that everyone will pay attention to him. If everyone shows interest in him, he is happy, and if they do not, he is not happy. We can always see this. Even a one-year-old like Kwon Jin does this. (Laughter) 
Such thoughts, ideologies, and emotions do not just disappear as we grow older. As we age and gain more experiences in life, we tend to cling more to those thoughts. 
And when looking at our Unification Church members, before thinking about the Unification Church, they tend to think of themselves first. They hope that the Unification Church will be for them and that the teacher will be for them. Is that not true? "Yes." 
The problem lies in where? Everyone wants to think only of themselves, but that cannot happen. It cannot happen, and it does not happen. Why does it not happen? 
You see, there is a standard for a meter, and if we take that standard and use it as a basis to align everything, then if something fits that standard, we no longer need to adjust it. If it breaks, we can adjust it, and then we can align everything else. Because the same representative has emerged, we can expand by aligning with that standard, creating the third representative, the fourth representative, and so on. 
What is the condition? It must be the same. It must be the same. It must be the same not only externally but also qualitatively and characteristically. Then we can truly say it is ideal. 
In the same way, whatever standard you have, whether centered on yourself, your family, your country, this world, or the universe, we hope to play around with it. That is what we desire and wish for, but why does it not happen? The issue is whether I can stand at the center of such a position in accordance with any principle. We can think about this. 
This applies to any individual, any family, any organization, including our Unification Church. We hope that the Unification Church and all of us will be centered around it. Then, there must be some model based on the Unification Church or religion, and there must be a standard that can be aligned with that model. If it is a nation, there must be a model that has all the necessary content centered around that nation and all the countries of the world. 
When you think about this, what is the existence that claims to be the center of this world? What is it? No matter how you think about it... could it be the animal world? How do you think? "No." Only humans can have such thoughts, only humans. 
Then, what other existence can think like that? If there is a God who is a superior being, then one might think that is possible. Is that not so? "Yes." Therefore, if there is a world and a spiritual realm, if there is a physical world and a spiritual world, we conclude that there are these two realms. Now, if we think this way, God must also think, "I want to be the center of the spiritual realm." 
Then, if God wants to be the center of the world and humans also want to be the center of the world, what will happen if these two beings both claim to be the center? If God says, "Let’s do it centered around me," and humans say, "Let’s do it centered around me," what will happen? If there is a couple, and the husband says, "I must be the center," and the wife also says, "I must be the center," what will happen? If both are in that position, a fight will inevitably break out. If both insist on being the center, a conflict will arise. 
If you stand in such a position, no matter how much God is, He will say, "What is this!" and will forcefully bring you down. However, that cannot happen. People may tell God to "get lost," but that cannot happen. So what will happen? Here, a mutual agreement arises. Therefore, it must be good for both you and me, and we must think of a way where both can be the center. That is the conclusion we must come to. Do you understand what that means? "Yes." 
Then what kind of agreement will we establish? "You exist for me, centered around me!" If we establish such an agreement, we will be eternally unhappy. There will only be eternal struggle. So, what kind of agreement must we establish? "I am the center for you. I exist for your benefit." Outside of this logic, we cannot find anything. 
Therefore, no matter how much you stand in the central position, you must say, "I am here for your benefit. If there is something good, it is not mine unless you are happy, and if there is happiness, I can only be happy if you are happy." If these conditions are met, everyone will agree. We cannot help but find this fundamental issue here, and when we look again at where all human happiness, joy, and ideals originate, we conclude that if it does not align with this principle, it is not an ideal, and if it does not align with this principle, it is not happiness. 
A being that prioritizes others must be at the center. 
Can you be happy alone? "No." No matter how much one is in the central position, what happiness can one find being alone? Even if I stand in the central position, when I am alone, I seek a place that is not alone. I go looking for it. Do you all agree? No matter how beautiful a woman is and how she has everything to be envied in the world, can she say, "I am the center" and be alone? Even if she has everything, when she is alone, where does she go? She goes back. Is that right? Why is that? Because it is not good. If it is not good, what happens? It sinks. It retreats. If it is good, what happens? It becomes evident. Does anyone ever say, "Everyone! Follow my loneliness!"? "No." Then what must it be? It must be good. One must promote what is good. 
When we see this, no matter how absolute God is, He cannot be alone. That is certain, right? "Yes." When we look at God centered around this, God also thinks, "I will be the center of the universe." However, if God establishes the logic, "All beings, you exist for me. Only then will I be happy," that would be a big problem. 
What we need to understand here is that for God to be the center, He must establish the condition, "I exist for you. I exist because of you," and then stand in the position of "I will take responsibility to remove all your unhappy circumstances." 
From this perspective, this world will inevitably be as it is. Then, when we look at God and humanity, for whom must God exist? God speaks through me.

Chesnoff and Nagorski: How is the Unification Church different from other Christian denominations?

Reverend Moon: The new revelation I have received clearly reveals God's will. What is that will? It is to save the world. The Unification Church is not just another denomination. The Unification Church is engaged in a movement to save the world. All those who participate in our movement clearly understand the concept of individuals centered on God, families centered on God, nations centered on God, and a world centered on God through God's word.

Question: How was God's will revealed to you?

At the age of 16, I had a deep spiritual experience of meeting Jesus in Korea. That was the beginning of the revelation. Since that special encounter, I have been in continuous dialogue with the living God and all the saints of the spirit world, including Jesus. 

Question: Why do you think God chose you?

God chose and ordained me according to His timetable. But why did He do that? That question must be asked directly to God. What I know for sure is that such a mission has been entrusted to me. Currently, God is facing three troublesome issues. What are they? First, the widespread problem of moral decay; second, the issue of rebuilding Christianity, which is fragmented and declining; and third, the growing power of communism, which is the force of Satan before God. In particular, communism is the greatest obstacle to building the kingdom on earth. These revelations have been completed in the "Principle of Creation," and I have developed a movement, which is the Unification Church.

Question: You speak as if you are a prophet, which also implies that you consider yourself the Messiah.

We are living in the era of a new Messiah. Two thousand years ago, Jesus Christ knew that calling himself the Messiah would not help him fulfill his mission, so he never spoke of it. I do not call myself the Messiah. I simply follow God's command faithfully.

Question: However, you do not exclude the possibility that you could be the Messiah.

Let God answer you directly about you and the world.

Question: You have emphasized that the returning Lord will appear as a married Korean person and that new ideas will come from Korea. Why Korea?

Korea is a nation chosen by God. Korea is divided. The confrontation at Panmunjom between the two sides is no different from the confrontation between the heavenly world and the satanic world. We must have the final confrontation in Korea. The victory of Korea, especially in the fight against communism, is not just Korea's. I came to this country to recreate that struggle in America. Until now, America has avoided its responsibility to the world. Didn't that happen in Vietnam? America is in a position to determine not only God's destiny but also the destiny of the world. Because God wants a champion. America bears the destiny of fighting communism on a global scale. Such ideological confrontation is inevitable.

Question: Do you have any connections with the Korean government or the Korean CIA?

That thought is clearly nonsense. Our movement is not one that receives instructions from the Korean government as a religious organization. In fact, people from the Korean government have obstructed our movement countless times in the past. Because we have contributed significantly to the Korean government, they must now acknowledge our achievements. We have conveyed the victory theory to over 20 million people through our pure efforts. However, that does not mean we have entered into a cooperative relationship with the Korean government. President Park is doing his job as president, and I am doing my job as a religious leader.

Question: Have you ever received support from anti-communist groups in Korea or around the world? For example, have you received support from people like Yoshio Kodama in Japan?

I have not received a single penny of support. I have never met Mr. Kodama or had any exchanges with him or his organization. Communists are spreading such rumors to tarnish our reputation.

Question: I understand that you have claimed, "I will conquer the world and make it submit. The day will naturally come when my words will be law." What is your political purpose?

I have no political purpose. Such statements are quoted without considering the context. People extract quotes from my long speeches that I give spontaneously, and they can be misinterpreted. There are also issues with translation.

Question: So, are you saying you have no intention of conquering the world?

Of course, in a political sense, that is true. God is the ruler of the world. And I do not place myself in God's position. However, God speaks through me, so the one who speaks is not Reverend Moon, but God. That is why so many young people follow me.

Question: Is placing your members in high positions in the government one of your goals?

That is not a matter for the church to be involved in, nor should it be under the church's control. However, as our membership continues to grow, excellent leaders may emerge from among them. That is welcome. However, I have no intention of seizing any political power for myself or my organization.

Question: You live in a $625,000 house as a billionaire businessman and own yachts that are always available for use. Is there any reason you hold such economic power?

God has blessed me. However, I am a religious leader, not a billionaire businessman. God has given me boundless blessings. People say that anything I touch turns to gold. To some extent, that is true. However, I know very well why God gives me such blessings. That is, God knows that even if He blesses me like that, it does not belong to Reverend Moon; not a penny goes into Reverend Moon's account. Everything I do is for God. If I were to gather young people to use them for myself, no one would follow me. However, they understand my honesty and dedicated life.

Question: What is the scale of the economic resources owned by the Unification Church around the world?

I do not know well. In reality, I do not keep track of how much church property there is. I have no interest in such things. I only provide spiritual guidance.

Question: Then who keeps track?

The leaders of each country do. There is no unified management system.

Question: I understand that Unification Church members live very frugally, but you live comfortably. Why is that?

I have lived very frugally for most of my life. However, now, whether I like it or not, I have become an international figure. Many people come to see me. So, there are also issues of protocol. Some people say that I need security and a certain level of environment.

Question: Is safety not guaranteed around you and your church? It sounds like you are speaking from a kind of obsession. Why do you emphasize safety?

I am fulfilling my mission as if I am walking on thin ice. I am under threat of life from communists. In fact, there have been many threats so far. As our movement becomes more active, there will be more organized plots to threaten my life. For example, Kim Il-sung of North Korea publicly states that Reverend Moon is the greatest obstacle to his revolutionary strategy. Those people do not realize that if this Reverend Moon disappears, countless new Reverend Moons will appear. There is no interruption in God's work.

Question: Why do your church and members persistently continue fundraising? What is the reason for emphasizing material things?

I do not deny material values. To serve God, such things are necessary. In order to realize God's ideals on earth, abundant resources are also needed.

Question: Why do you not donate anything to solve the hunger problem in Africa, for example?

We also engage in social work. In the future, many people will receive help, and currently, poor people and orphans are receiving assistance.
Please understand that this is a fact. My special mission is to guide people to know God.

Q: I hear that your factory in Korea produces weapons. Is that true?  
Our machine factory is contracted to produce a certain amount of weapons. In Korea, it is a national obligation. And there is no large corporation that does not participate in such defense industries. We have a contract that states that 5 to 10 percent of what we produce must be for national defense.

Q: What kinds of weapons have you produced?  
That is information handled by the government, but we have produced minor parts of weapons.

Q: Are you planning to establish factories in the United States and Europe, just like in Korea and Japan?  
Yes. We are particularly interested in Germany, which can be considered the heart of Europe. We must save Germany from communism.

Q: There are claims that you brainwash your congregation...  
I received similar questions when I spoke to the members of the National Assembly of this country. At that time, I answered, "Are you saying that the American people are so foolish as to be brainwashed by Reverend Moon, a Korean? Moreover, I am giving a speech through an interpreter!" The young people who come to our church are not that foolish. They are smart, idealistic, and strong-minded young people. Therefore, when they come to know God's power and love, they are drawn to it like a magnet. Our doors are open 24 hours a day. Anyone can come in, and anyone can leave.

Q: You emphasize the importance of family, but doesn't that lead to discord among family members?  
If a member of the Unification Church abandons their parents, that person is not a true member. A true member would honor their parents. Many young people are abandoned in their families. They are longing for love. When they join our movement, they are impressed and come to know what happiness is. For the first time, they meet people they can believe in and love. So they become members and follow us in reality. Some of their parents may become jealous of this, while others have no objection except for the fact that their sons and daughters are following me, who came from Korea.

Q: Have you ever been ordained by other established churches?  
Just as many prophets in history have been ordained by God, so have I. I talk to God every day. The living God is with me. There is no better ordination than that.

Communism, centered on materialism, denies God and denies the original centrality, so it is a worldview that is purely focused on the physical body. God's Will

Today, I will speak on the topic of "God's Will." 

When we see countless religious people practicing their faith, we can understand that regardless of the religion, they are all looking toward one world, one will centered around God.

God is the central being of the universe, the master of the created world, and the Father of humanity. Therefore, the will of God is the most important issue. So, what is God's will? Today, theologians may see it as both an extremely simple question and an extremely difficult one. At one time, I invited a prominent theologian from Korea to a training session for local leaders in Korea, and we discussed the question of what God's will is. At that time, the answer was, "It is the easiest and the hardest."

Ultimately, to know God's will, we must understand who God is. God is the center of the universe and the master of all creation. Do you know this? "Yes." Do you believe it, do you understand it? "Yes." Then, who is God? "He is our human Father." This is an amazing answer. Ultimately, God is the central being of the universe, the master of the created world, and our human Father.

How did this come to be? Why is it so? For such things to come into existence (pointing to the table), there must be a central being in the world of existence. We cannot deny this.

For example, when we look at a household, we see that all the household items are uniquely shaped in various forms, and we understand that there is a master, a central being in that house.

Now, what did that master and central being create all these things for? Ultimately, it is for living, for sustenance.... How do we live? God created an environment called family, dreaming of a place where He could live with His children in love. This leads us to the conclusion that we must live in such a way.

Ultimately, if there is a master and a central being, then all the household items created by that central being are for sustenance, to make life comfortable. And the things that exist for living are not just for themselves. If there is a son, it is for the son; if there is a wife, one cannot help but create or buy things that the wife would like. If someone truly loves their children or their wife, they will naturally buy things that their loved ones would enjoy. This is how it works. When you go to your homes, you see that because there are parents, when a father buys something, he usually buys what the mother and children would like. This is a common-sense conclusion.

Now, if God created heaven and earth, did He create it for Himself to enjoy, or did He create it for His beloved children to enjoy? From this perspective, we can deduce that God created it for the sake of His children rather than for Himself. Then, from the viewpoint of who should be the master of all creation, we can infer that God would prefer that the master of all creation be His beloved objects. So, who is that beloved object? When we say it is humanity, it means that all things were created for God, but ultimately, there is a higher dimension of meaning centered around love.

From this perspective, when you know God.... God is the center of the universe, the master of all creation, and our Father. If you truly know God, have you ever thought that all of heaven and earth is "for me, mine"? Have you thought about that? When your mother or father buys you even one piece of clothing, like a tie, you boast, saying, "Ah, my mom bought this for me." How much do you boast when they buy you a piece of clothing? What is the value of that? It is not much. Moreover, it is not something your mother or father made; it was bought at a store.

Whoosh, whoosh..." and everything came into being. (Laughter) If so, it is seen that there is no value in love; it means that there is no value in love.
